\"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java\", \"symbol\": \"ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Apache Kafka implements a comprehensive Java-based plugin/extension loading system in the Connect framework, centered around interface-based dependency injection and reflective plugin discovery.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Isolation System\\n\\nThe plugin isolation mechanism is built on three key classloader components:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first classloading semantics for plugin isolation. Each plugin gets loaded in its own classloader to prevent conflicts with shared dependencies.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A parent classloader that delegates to isolated PluginClassLoaders while maintaining child-first delegation for plugins. It manages a map of discovered plugins and their classloaders.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** and **PluginClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java and PluginClassLoaderFactory.java): Factories that create instances of these classloaders, with support for mocking in tests.\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery System\\n\\nThe system supports two plugin discovery mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Uses ClassGraph library to scan classpath for classes implementing plugin interfaces at runtime. This provides comprehensive discovery but has higher computational cost.\\n\\n2. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism with META-INF/services manifest files. Faster but requires explicit manifest entries.\\n\\nBoth scanners extend **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java), which provides the common discovery framework.\\n\\n## Plugin Type System\\n\\n**PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java) is an enumeration defining the plugin categories:\\n- SOURCE (SourceConnector)\\n- SINK (SinkConnector)\\n- CONVERTER (Converter)\\n- HEADER_CONVERTER (HeaderConverter)\\n- TRANSFORMATION (Transformation)\\n- PREDICATE (Predicate)\\n- CONFIGPROVIDER (ConfigProvider)\\n- REST_EXTENSION (ConnectRestExtension)\\n- CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY (ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy)\\n\\n## Plugin Metadata and Results\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): A generic descriptor class that holds metadata about a discovered plugin including class reference, version, type, and classloader.\\n\\n2. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Aggregates SortedSets of PluginDesc objects for each plugin type, representing the complete discovery result.\\n\\n3. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, JAR hierarchy, or class hierarchy) with its associated URLs and classloader.\\n\\n## Interface-Based Plugin System\\n\\nThe plugin system uses interface-based dependency injection for nine key plugin types:\\n\\n1. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base interface for connectors, with subclasses:\\n   - **SourceConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java)\\n   - **SinkConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java)\\n\\n2. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for converting between Kafka Connect data format and serialized bytes.\\n\\n3. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Specialized converter for Kafka message headers.\\n\\n4. **Transformation** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java): Generic interface for single message transformations.\\n\\n5. **Predicate** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java): Interface for predicates that determine when transformations apply.\\n\\n6. **ConfigProvider** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/provider/ConfigProvider.java): Interface for providing configuration data from external sources.\\n\\n7. **ConnectRestExtension** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java): Interface for extending Connect REST API with custom resources.\\n\\n8. **ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java): Interface for enforcing policies on client config overrides.\\n\\n9. **Task** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Task.java): Base for SourceTask and SinkTask with associated record and context types.\\n\\n## Configuration and Dependency Injection\\n\\nAll plugins implement **Configurable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java), which provides a single configure(Map<String, ?>) method for dependency injection. Plugins may optionally implement **Monitorable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/metrics/Monitorable.java) to register custom metrics.\\n\\n## Plugin Instantiation and Classloader Management\\n\\n**Plugins** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) is the central manager that:\\n- Discovers and maintains plugin descriptors\\n- Instantiates plugins with appropriate classloaders\\n- Manages classloader context switching via **LoaderSwap** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java)\\n- Supports versioned plugin loading\\n- Provides plugin recommendations via **PluginsRecommenders** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java)\\n\\n## Utility and Infrastructure\\n\\n1. **PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java): Provides utilities for:\\n   - implements a comprehensive Java-based plugin/extension loading system in the Connect framework, centered around interface-based dependency injection and reflective plugin discovery.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Isolation System\\n\\nThe plugin isolation mechanism is built on three key classloader components:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first classloading semantics for plugin isolation. Each plugin gets loaded in its own classloader to prevent conflicts with shared dependencies.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A parent classloader that delegates to isolated PluginClassLoaders while maintaining child-first delegation for plugins. It manages a map of discovered plugins and their classloaders.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** and **PluginClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java and PluginClassLoaderFactory.java): Factories that create instances of these classloaders, with support for mocking in tests.\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery System\\n\\nThe system supports two plugin discovery mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Uses ClassGraph library to scan classpath for classes implementing plugin interfaces at runtime. This provides comprehensive discovery but has higher computational cost.\\n\\n2. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism with META-INF/services manifest files. Faster but requires explicit manifest entries.\\n\\nBoth scanners extend **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java), which provides the common discovery framework.\\n\\n## Plugin Type System\\n\\n**PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java) is an enumeration defining the plugin categories:\\n- SOURCE (SourceConnector)\\n- SINK (SinkConnector)\\n- CONVERTER (Converter)\\n- HEADER_CONVERTER (HeaderConverter)\\n- TRANSFORMATION (Transformation)\\n- PREDICATE (Predicate)\\n- CONFIGPROVIDER (ConfigProvider)\\n- REST_EXTENSION (ConnectRestExtension)\\n- CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY (ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy)\\n\\n## Plugin Metadata and Results\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): A generic descriptor class that holds metadata about a discovered plugin including class reference, version, type, and classloader.\\n\\n2. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Aggregates SortedSets of PluginDesc objects for each plugin type, representing the complete discovery result.\\n\\n3. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, JAR hierarchy, or class hierarchy) with its associated URLs and classloader.\\n\\n## Interface-Based Plugin System\\n\\nThe plugin system uses interface-based dependency injection for nine key plugin types:\\n\\n1. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base interface for connectors, with subclasses:\\n   -
